
-----title

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　丁忧居家，有诗咏怀。作品：《忧居杜门久废笔砚兹因卜筑辄有所感不免破戒作数语呈诸亲友》<div id='poem_101840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忧居杜门久废笔砚兹因卜筑辄有所感不免破戒作数语呈诸亲友</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101840")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101840'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101840'>平生事幽讨，性与山水便。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101840'>晚岁辟三径，颇喜得地偏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101840'>远不去桑梓，近与松楸连。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101840'>青山枕其后，流水绕其前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101840'>群山更簇簇，左右相周旋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101840'>栋宇虽未立，气象已足观。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101840'>旁人笑我拙，空囊无一钱。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101840'>何苦欲架屋，作此烦恼缘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101840'>我岂不自知，老去将终焉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101840'>游居与寝卧，安可无数椽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101840'>人生七十稀，自古尝有言。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101840'>我今五十七，髭鬓已皤然。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101840'>纵使此身健，前去能几年。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101840'>仕宦虽龃龉，亦复忝蕃宣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101840'>向来为亲养，犹或强著鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101840'>今既成永感，前事都弃捐。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101840'>傥或未死灭，誓将老林泉。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101840'>遂此卜筑志，闭门日高眠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101840'>栽花满我屋，种竹环我园。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101840'>山上创一堂，湖中具一船。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101840'>从容与亲旧，取次中圣贤。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101840'>虽无万钟禄，虽无二顷田。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101840'>胸中富丘壑，眼界饱风烟。<div id='poem_sentence_22_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_101840'>自足了一世，此外休问天。<div id='poem_sentence_23_101840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_101840'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_101840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　丁忧居家，有诗再和前韵。作品：《再和》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年11月</a>　十一月，权户部侍郎兼权知临安府钱端礼荐其才。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='209aa3f4fc164b15ab4eb0222f9f4c5c_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1167')">1165-1167年</a>，62-64岁</div><div id='209aa3f4fc164b15ab4eb0222f9f4c5c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　六月十九日，除敷文阁直学士提举太平兴国宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年3月</a>　提举太平兴国宫。春，有诗咏怀。作品：《丙戌送春有作》《和送春诗送陈泽民》<div id='poem_101812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙戌送春有作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101812")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101812'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101812'>三月三十日，春去人尽惜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101812'>我独惜春多，欲留春不得。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101812'>忆昨仕行都，亦屡逢春色。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101812'>王事多鞅掌，常苦无暇隙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101812'>担上看桃李，负春长叹息。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101812'>每欲早归田，恨不生羽翼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101812'>及至今得归，亦复少欢适。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101812'>平生无室庐，方且事工役。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101812'>老妻病累年，年来觉转剧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101812'>百事总关心，十日九不怿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101812'>把酒对东风，一春能几夕。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101812'>因念梦幻躯，处世不满百。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101812'>今日六十三，已是桑榆迫。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101812'>纵使到七十，能得几年客。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101812'>幸春有旧好，一笑常莫逆。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101812'>今既舍我归，动是经年隔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101812'>聊复倒离樽，与春话胸臆。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101812'>我方葺园亭，随分足泉石。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101812'>准拟共东君，著此几两屐。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101812'>丁宁春早回，莫使常相忆。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101812'>今宵已拚醉，坐待东方白。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101812'>明旦各分飞，断肠芳草碧。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101812'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_101812_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和送春诗送陈泽民</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101879")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101879'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101879'>少年买青春，千金初不惜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101879'>常恐春不留，韶华难再得。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101879'>种杏更栽桃，为春添景色。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101879'>对酒复当歌，与春亡间隙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101879'>春去或未来，日探春消息。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101879'>及至春又归，送春恨无翼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101879'>追随九十日，无日不自适。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101879'>胡为把一麾，千里从吏役。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101879'>当涂古道院，事简非繁剧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101879'>宴坐对江山，亦足自怡怿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101879'>所叹乏游从，无与共良夕。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101879'>陈侯有高标，鸷鸟空累百。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101879'>落笔动成篇，端不在促迫。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101879'>不意牢落中，乃得此佳客。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101879'>人事苦参商，天意有顺逆。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101879'>笑言犹未竟，遽尔成乖隔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101879'>虽未唱阳关，别恨已填臆。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101879'>此邦固寂寥，颇亦富水石。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101879'>方拟出郊坰，共试登山屐。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101879'>何事逐春归，不念人相忆。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101879'>春事虽已阑，残花尚红白。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101879'>且复引离尊，倒此香醪碧。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101879'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_101879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年4月</a>　春，起知太平州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7d588a2383d840e9af640a420663f4bc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月21日</a>　将到家乡，有诗感怀。作品：《六月二十一日早行十六首》<div id='poem_100954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_100954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_100953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_100953'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_100953'>稻苗初穗出纷纷，半是青云半白云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_100953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_100953'>坐看黄云呈上瑞，田家无处不忻忻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_100953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_100951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_100951'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_100951'>为忆湖山且暂归，此心不是要追时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_100951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_100951'>君恩留我非由己，寄语山灵莫勒移。<div id='poem_sentence_1_100951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101797'>向来苦宦游，颇恨归不早。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101797'>复值君诞辰，满目春光好。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101797'>我方务清虚，志不在金宝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　有诗与乡人唱和。作品：《耿曼老将命乡邦见过匆遽言别复作诗送之》<div id='poem_101955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_101955'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101955'>我方退老湖山上，混迹渔樵甘放浪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101955'>亲旧凋零会面稀，与君亦复成疏旷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101955'>何期拥节到乡邦，得得驱车肯迂访。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101955'>开门倒屣笑相迎，尽室欢忻无此况。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101955'>湖光山色似争辉，两眼韶华更骀荡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101955'>伸眉抵掌话中肠，正好花前倒春酿。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101955'>胡为欲去挽不留，忍把阳关容易唱。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101955'>嗟乎来日苦无多，况是频年婴拙恙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101955'>兴来亦欲强登临，龙钟未免扶藜杖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101955'>目前衰飒已如斯，宁保明年见花放。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101955'>而今花下幸逢君，岂容不尽长鲸量。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101955'>如君志尚迥不群，治行既高心且壮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101955'>方当圣主急搜扬，为斲岂应遗巧匠。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101970'>几年欲作冥鸿举，今日方随倦鸟还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101970'>有水不妨时载月，无人谁与共登山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101970'>相望千里空相忆，尊酒何时一破颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101354'>五禽聊作林间戏，双鲤忽传江上书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101354'>诗句方惭成间断，交情岂谓益勤渠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101354_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101354'>开缄更诵惊人语，恍若相从听佩琚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101355'>但恐赐环来北阙，不容拄笏看西山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101355'>祇今汲直如公少，正赖忠言一犯颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101355'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101355_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101572' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101572' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101572?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_101572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101572'>感君不替绸缪意，使我还销鄙吝心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101572'>他日相逢重把酒，莫辞蘸甲十分深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101572'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101572_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1173')">1172-1173年</a>　奉祠居里。有诗抒怀。作品：《答客难》《闻同庚不幸有感》《览洛中名园记有感》《感花》《癸巳岁邑中大歉三七侄捐金散谷以济艰食因成三十韵以纪之》《感旧》<div id='poem_101975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101975?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答客难</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101975")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101975'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101975'>我治湖上园，占断山水窟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101975'>幽事日相关，颇觉无暇逸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101975'>有客来相过，云欲救我失。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101975'>谓我虽爱閒，未得居閒术。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101975'>众人役利名，公独役景物。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101975'>固与众人殊，未免俱汩没。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101975'>孰若淡无营，燕坐一虚室。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101975'>百念尽消除，百事付真率。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101975'>物来则应之，岂可自撄拂。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101975'>客言非不忠，我意客未悉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101975'>万物仗境生，百果因花实。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101975'>我闻洛阳城，名园浑比迹。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101975'>至如司马公，朴素世莫及。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101975'>有园号独乐，晚岁亦加葺。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101975'>人心固不同，岂能尽如一。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101975'>顾我病且衰，行年将七十。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101975'>光景去不留，馀龄那可必。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101975'>要当且逍遥，乐此桑榆日。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101975'>宁如土木偶，终朝长兀兀。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101975'>况有佳山水，兹焉久蟠郁。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101975'>地灵尽发露，一旦为我出。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101975'>若不一领略，无乃太拘执。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101975'>何妨几席间，时与相顾揖。<div id='poem_sentence_22_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_101975'>择胜把酒杯，搜奇入诗笔。<div id='poem_sentence_23_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_101975'>犹恨景物多，未能尽收拾。<div id='poem_sentence_24_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_101975'>他人视若忙，我心常自佚。<div id='poem_sentence_25_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_101975'>人无所用心，先圣每忿疾。<div id='poem_sentence_26_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_101975'>既不学群儿，诧仙仍佞佛。<div id='poem_sentence_27_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_101975'>不有博奕乎，为之犹胜弗。<div id='poem_sentence_28_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_101975'>客既闻斯言，语塞几若讷。<div id='poem_sentence_29_101975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_101975'>因为客书之，聊以志彷佛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101948'>湖山堪寓目，风月足怡神。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101948'>有花我共醉，有鸟助我吟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101948'>若不自娱乐，开口对芳辰。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101230'>岂料青春今过半，萧萧风雨却愁人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101230'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_101230_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101233?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_101233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101233'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101233'>嗟我明年是七旬，此生能见几番春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101233'>凭谁为补青天漏，放出春光处处新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101233'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_101233_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101231?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_101231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101231'>一雨绵绵不暂停，天公于此底无情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101231'>不应直待花飘尽，始放阳和作好晴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101231'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_101231_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸巳岁邑中大歉三七侄捐金散谷以济艰食因成三十韵以纪之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101939")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101939'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101939'>吾家谓侄非常儿，自幼读书尝下帷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101939'>平居事母尽孝道，力供子职曾无违。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101939'>辛勤农亩三十载，顿立门户成家肥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101939'>耻同流俗事骄吝，好贤乐业常怡怡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101939'>闻人急难如在己，见义踊跃无不为。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101939'>造桥砌路未为德，折券释逋未足奇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101939'>究其存心用意处，尤在邑人艰食时。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101939'>此邑山多土田少，民贫自昔难支持。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101939'>其间岁收数百斛，已为富室他可知。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101939'>况复今年苦亢旱，州里远近咸告饥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101939'>田畴弥望总如燎，细民未免俱流移。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101939'>纵使人能保常产，亦复有甑无米炊。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101939'>虽幸朝家行赈济，正恐未能遍群黎。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101939'>往往倾村走山谷，荷锄掘地寻蕨萁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101939'>取根为粉虽可饱，食之既久人亦羸。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101939'>春来必至生疫疠，死填沟壑夫何疑。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101939'>吾侄见之轸忧恻，首议倡率输家赀。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101939'>既捐青蚨二百万，犹恨籴贵难疗饥。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101939'>庾中仅存二千石，一旦倾倒尽散之。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101939'>此心但欲济邻里，身外浮名非所希。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101939'>吁嗟薄俗务贪鄙，计较升斗争刀锥。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101939'>徒知富有可润屋，岂虑人怨亲戚离。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101939'>有如吾侄为此举，吾乡自古应亦稀。<div id='poem_sentence_22_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_101939'>小惠所施固未博，风义自足洗浇漓。<div id='poem_sentence_23_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_101939'>傥使人人皆若尔，千里岂复忧馁时。<div id='poem_sentence_24_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_101939'>第愿吾侄广此意，所为尽从今日推。<div id='poem_sentence_25_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_101939'>阴功在人天心报，会俾尔寿膺繁禧。<div id='poem_sentence_26_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_101939'>梓里遗芳传未艾，世有子孙攀桂枝。<div id='poem_sentence_27_101939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_101939'>岂惟同里共歆艳，亦使吾侄<span id='poem_sentence_4_101777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101376")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101376'>已是年龄及七旬，田园稍给未全贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101376'>儿孙初识传儒业，世俗还称作贵人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101376'>门外湖山浑可乐，沙头鸥鹭更相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101376'>莫将尘事干吾虑，已向君王乞此身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_101386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101386'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101386'>坐阅流年已七旬，从前忧道不忧贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101386'>肯教世指为痴汉，只愿乡称作善人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101386'>老去固应忘物我，归来岂是负君亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101386'>尝闻知进须知退，庶得终全不辱身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101385'>每对青山常意适，才逢白叟便情亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101385'>静中百念俱灰灭<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作减，据仙居本改）</span>，识破浮生梦幻身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101385_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_101384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101384'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101384'>封章上达已经旬，所乞原非为贱贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101384'>七秩自知非久客，一心只欲作闲人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　奉祠居里。有诗与友人叶性之唱和。作品：《和叶性之喜雨》<div id='poem_101435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101435")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101435'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101435'>去岁饥荒特异常，那知今日便丰穰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101435'>田畴雨足经时润，院宇风生着处凉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101435'>老去我方辞五斗，秋来谁解积千仓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101435'>从今闾里无艰食，会见家家酒熟香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101435'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　妻郭氏七十生朝，以诗抒怀。作品：《老妻生朝为寿》<div id='poem_101363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>老妻生朝为寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101363")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101363'>人生七十古来稀，我幸君今及见之。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101363'>教得子能传素业，养成孙亦守清规。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101363'>禀生坎坷今当泰，积善初终志不移。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101363'>白首喜为林下伴，愿从今日到期颐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101363'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101363_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　致仕居里。生活闲适，有诗送津赴任。作品：《送津儿之官丽水》<div id='poem_101942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送津儿之官丽水</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101942")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101942'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101942'>忆我初仕时，不敢望高位。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101942'>但得宰一同，便可行己志。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101942'>实惠傥及民，死亦有生气。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101942'>况复著阴功，子孙将不坠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101942'>胡为人惮之，百计欲求避。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101942'>我闻事无难，辞难岂为义。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101942'>世路虽多艰，官途须历试。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101942'>是用俾吾儿，往当民社寄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101942'>眷言古括州，山水有佳致。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101942'>我尚记昔年，尝为郡守贰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101942'>虽无德在人，人亦安平易。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101942'>百里闻汝来，想见多忻慰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101942'>要当尽此心，有以塞其意。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101942'>诚能使吏民，自此知怀畏。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101942'>家家各安居，人人共称治。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101942'>纵或罹谤伤，固自有公议。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101942'>有如汝所存，俯仰似无愧。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101942'>功名馀事耳，何必成与遂。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101942'>年来我挂冠，方得闲中味。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101942'>无乃逼桑榆，七十仍有二。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101942'>知复几何时，得见汝娱侍。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101942'>虽幸枕湖山，已辟幽栖地。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101942'>有诗谁伴吟，有酒谁同醉。<div id='poem_sentence_22_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_101942'>正欲汝相随，俄然又相离。<div id='poem_sentence_23_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_101942'>会须早归来，日作斑衣戏。<div id='poem_sentence_24_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_101942'>个中有真乐，岂必三旌贲。<div id='poem_sentence_25_101942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_101942'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_101942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　致仕居里。有诗感怀。作品：《予与王瞻叔韩通一林梅卿余知默徐彦才六人皆同庚也一登政路五上禁涂其四久已物故所存者独知默与予耳今日得报知默又已云亡念年齿至此予亦岂久于世者乎怅然有感于怀因成数语以自解》<div id='poem_101809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予与王瞻叔韩通一林梅卿余知默徐彦才六人皆同庚也一登政路五上禁涂其四久已物故所存者独知默与予耳今日得报知默又已云亡念年齿至此予亦岂久于世者乎怅然有感于怀因成数语以自解</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101809")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101809'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101809'>同庚非不多，达者能有几。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101809'>七十二年间，六人而已矣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101809'>其四迹已陈，止予二人尔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101809'>今朝闻讣音，其一又不起。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101809'>嗟予独何人，偶尔未见鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101809'>自度如许衰，宁久红尘里。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101809'>念此梦幻身，谁能保终始。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101809'>失者虽或非，得亦未为是。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101809'>死者固可悲，生亦不足喜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101809'>幸然已挂冠，万事不到耳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101809'>何妨日凭栏，乐此佳山水。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101809'>仍更日开尊，赏此新桃李。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101809'>时时命歌童，唱个陶真理。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101809'>倘或未溘然，亦足娱暮齿。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101809'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_101809_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年12月</a>　致仕居里。有文。作品：《朱氏旌表门闾碑》<div id='poem_1243254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱氏旌表门闾碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_1243254")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243254'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243254'>淳熙二年，今皇帝以太上皇帝寿登七秩，亘古无有，思鸿厥庆，施于臣庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243254_comment'></div>乃十有二月赦文：孝行节义著于乡闾者，长吏以闻，当议旌录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243254_comment'></div>先是元年正月，台州守臣詹仪之奏，州之仕者暨士民凡百一十有七人，合词言临海县贡士朱伯履妻陈氏有节行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243254_comment'></div>伯履早世，年盛子幼，媒氏请复有行，陈氏抚膺恸绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243254_comment'></div>既苏，叹曰：「吾宁速死，忍闻此言」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243254_comment'></div>引刀欲自剪，侍婢亟持之，乃免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243254_comment'></div>事父母、舅姑至孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243254_comment'></div>姑宜人林氏年高齿豁，陈氏手调旨甘，动能顺适其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243254_comment'></div>姑垂绝，执其手曰：「愿妇子孙寿数如我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243254_comment'></div>训二子希尹、希牧有法，以文行、孝友称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243254_comment'></div>陈氏年九十有三，齿发不衰，姆则壸彝，州里所矜式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243254_comment'></div>天产祥嘏，厥有桃实、萱颖之异，请以其事列诸朝，特加褒表，以为节孝劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243254_comment'></div>州遣吏按验如状，谨以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243254_comment'></div>十月，守臣赵汝愚继剡上，皆未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243254_comment'></div>会庆礼行，耆年高节悉加崇奖，邦人援以为请，守臣尤袤申前奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243254_comment'></div>上嘉其节，明年三月壬戌，有旨特封安人，旌表门闾，仍宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243254_comment'></div>诏书至，阖郡欢迎，耋稚竦观，植门建台，诹协令式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243254_comment'></div>台成，有白雀翔于上，见者异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243254_comment'></div>一日希尹、希牧踵门曰：「母氏之节亦既列于赞书，诏于太史矣，愿公勒诸石，益为不朽传」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243254_comment'></div>芾辞不获命，则进二君而言曰：予昔与君之诸父游，习闻君家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243254_comment'></div>君之祖母林宜人治家以礼法，教子以义方，聚族千指，内外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243254_comment'></div>宜人年百有一岁，时郡守宗公颖欲请表其门，会颖去，弗果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243254_comment'></div>善积益丰，委址厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243254_comment'></div>安人实太子詹事陈公良翰之姊，风节义概，濡染素熟，承姑慈训，厥德惟肖，庸能身享上寿，保有全节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243254_comment'></div>方圣上以孝理天下，湛恩下逮，首承天宠，为世世万子孙光耀，且俾乡之为妇为母者以安人为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243254_comment'></div>今君又克顺承侈大之，是皆可书也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243254_comment'></div>予既纪其略，而又系之以诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243254_comment'></div>诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1243254'>妇德之修，至隐而昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243254_comment'></div>行成于家，而列于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243254_comment'></div>国有劝惩，赏罚而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243254_comment'></div>孰观而化，表厥宅里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243254_comment'></div>淑哉若人，识明志坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243254_comment'></div>之死靡它，不贰所天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243254_comment'></div>节则高矣，报亦云侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243254_comment'></div>既畀以年，庸介尔祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243254_comment'></div>嶪嶪崇台，左右其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243254_comment'></div>匪台之崇，维德之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1243254_comment'></div>诏而子孙，勿替勿懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1243254_comment'></div>永言保之，毋俾台坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1243254_comment'></div>告而里闾，而妇而母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1243254_comment'></div>惟节惟孝，惟台之视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1243254_comment'></div>圣孝不匮，善推所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1243254_comment'></div>我诗于石，垂世作规。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1243254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1177')">1176-1177年</a>　致仕居里。生活闲适。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　致仕居里。有诗咏怀。作品：《和陶读山海经十三首韵送机简堂自景星岩再住隐静》、（卷一）、、《和陶挽歌词三首》《病中有作》《述怀》<div id='poem_101905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和陶读山海经十三首韵送机简堂自景星岩再住隐静<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101905")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101905'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101905'>我年七十五，木末挂残阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101905'>纵使身未逝，亦岂能久长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101905'>尚冀林间住，与师共末光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101905'>孤云俄暂出，道俗纷苍黄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101905'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101905_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101908?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101908'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101908'>我自归林下，亦复与世疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101908'>赖有善知识，时能过吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101908'>伴我说道话，我爱读佛书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101908'>师为岩上去，我亦为膏车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101908'>便欲展我钵，随师同饭蔬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101908'>脱此尘俗累，长与岩石俱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101908'>此岩固高矣，卓出山海图。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101908'>但比吾师高，还恐岩不如。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101908'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_101908_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101907' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101907' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101907?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_101907'>我生山窟里，终朝面孱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101907'>独此岩未到，抱恨知几年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101907'>兹游信奇绝，一览小众山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101907'>更得师为主，二妙为易言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101907'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101907_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101910?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101910'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101910'>幽栖非不胜，触目是林丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101910'>若比兹岩秀，培塿固难俦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101910'>云山千里见，石泉四时流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101910'>登临有如此，何必更他游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101910'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101910_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_101911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101911'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101911'>爱山端有素，拘俗亦可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101911'>昨守当涂郡，不识隐静山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101911'>羡师来又去，愧我复何言。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101911'>尚期无久住，归送我残年。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101906_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101542?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101542'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101542'>扶疏岩下树，入夏总成阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101542'>人生多聚散，离别忽惊心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101542'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101542_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_101914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101914'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101914'>我与师来往，岁月虽未长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101914'>相看成二老，风流亦异常。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101914'>既宴坐岩上，我方为聚粮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101914'>傥师能早归，此乐犹未央。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101904'>求其道德尊，如师盖希有。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101904'>愿傅上乘人，永光临济后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101904'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101904_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101912?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101912'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101912'>吾邑多缁徒，浩浩若云海。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101912'>大机久已亡，赖有小机在。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101912'>乃更与一岑，纯全两无悔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101912'>堂堂二老禅，海内共期待。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101912'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101912_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_101909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101909'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101909'>古无住持事，但只传法旨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101909'>有能悟色空，便可超生死。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101909'>庸僧昧本原，岂识西归履。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101909'>买帖坐禅床，佛法将何恃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101915'>僧中有高僧，士亦有高士。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101915'>我虽不为高，心粗能知止。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101915'>师是个中人，特患不为尔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101915'>何幸我与师，俱是邻家子。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101915'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101915_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101913?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101913'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101913'>师本穷和尚，我亦穷秀才。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101913'>忍穷俱已彻，老肯不归来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101913'>今师虽暂别，泉石莫相猜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101913'>应缘聊复耳，师岂有心哉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/101902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和陶挽歌词三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101902")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101902'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101902'>吾年七十五，寿命不为促。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101902'>仕仅五十年，出处粗可录。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101902'>人生会有尽，自应身就木。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101902'>寄语亲旧辈，不必为我哭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101902'>百年如一梦，吾梦今始觉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101902'>亦既了万缘，无殆亦无辱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101902'>所欠惟一死，得死今已足。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101902'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_101902_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101901?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101901'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101901'>嗟我在生日，一饮数十觞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101901'>有时无酒饮，亦复泼醅尝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101901'>今日虽有酒，罗列在我傍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101901'>对之徒自叹，与世隔风光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101901'>所幸埋骨地，不离云外乡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101901'>魂魄时一游，此乐犹未央。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101901'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_101901_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101900?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101900'>老眼日昏昏，华发日萧萧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101900'>不死竟何待，理合葬荒郊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101900'>荒郊何所有，四面俱岧峣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101900'>荣木望秋落，亦已成枯条。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101900'>青松为我夕，白石为我朝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101900'>仍幸二亲墓，相去无几何。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101900'>今得从之游，欢喜如还家。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101900'>我心既欢喜，安用挽者歌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101900'>有人来奠我，但问山之阿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101900'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_101900_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中有作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101952")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101952'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101952'>吾年七十五，一朝忽患疟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101952'>仍害及老妻，对床更撼铎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101952'>寒时寒如冰，热后热如灼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101952'>既去还复来，如与我有约。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101952'>连日莫能休，尽室皆惊愕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101952'>饮啖一不忺，形骸顿如削。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101952'>细思岂无因，良由赋分薄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101952'>本是农家子，只合事耕作。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101952'>既已得美官，复有归田乐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101952'>已是无福当，又不知惭怍。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101952'>遂至疟鬼憎，故意来相虐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101952'>作诗告天公，纵我有过恶。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101952'>愿天少垂怜，疾痛且阔略。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101952'>但速赐之死，莫令我知觉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101952'>一生缠世网，正欲解其缚。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101952'>假使寿百年，宁免此一著。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101952'>不如早归藏，且免论强弱。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101952'>我非畏死人，久已办棺椁。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101952'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_101952_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>述怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101933")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101933'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101933'>我爱白乐天，千载共称贤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101933'>行年七十五，奄忽遂溘先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101933'>我爱范忠宣，一代名德全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101933'>年龄甫至此，亦复成弃捐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101933'>二公虽已逝，四海至今传。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101933'>顾我百无事，幸及二公年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101933'>今夏疾疢作，已分归黄泉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101933'>偶然得无事，固荷天见怜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101933'>但我有一语，恰欲与天言。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101933'>有生则有死，如行者言旋。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101933'>我是久行客，亦自应息肩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101933'>念人处一世，动为世网缠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101933'>开口罕欢笑，触绪多忧煎。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101933'>纵使至百岁，终困尘俗缘。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101933'>不如早瞑目，庶以全吾天。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101933'>是非与宠辱，总不到我前。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101933'>一心亦安静，却得返自然。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101933'>况我办归计，久已卜新阡<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《湖山集》卷三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101933'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_101933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　是年作《自祭文》<div id='poem_1243255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_1243255")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243255'>岁在戊戌，律应黄钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243255_comment'></div>寒云翳目，古木号风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243255_comment'></div>疏棂霜透，虚室尘蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243255_comment'></div>湖山居士，乃于是月，舍其旧宅，归于幽宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243255_comment'></div>亲戚伤其永诀，而相送于山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243255_comment'></div>酒在斝而虽旨，肴在俎而虽丰，但闻笳鼓，莫睹音容，于乎哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243255_comment'></div>我自幼为田舍儿，偶因把卷，遂免扶犁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243255_comment'></div>既参末宦，四十七期，入陪两禁，出把六麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243255_comment'></div>虽无玷缺，为人所嗤，第念报国，曾乏毫釐，不应叨冒，度越等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243255_comment'></div>复虑狷介，不能脂韦，久而不退，必触祸机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243255_comment'></div>旁无寸援，救之者谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243255_comment'></div>赖我此心，不昧神祇，迨至晚节，乃得放归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243255_comment'></div>既归林下，获脱絷羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243255_comment'></div>终日笑傲，饮酒赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1243255_comment'></div>山湖照映，妻子追随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1243255_comment'></div>时拿小艇，游于涟漪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1243255_comment'></div>临风对月，其乐无涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1243255_comment'></div>自顾何德，福至于斯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1243255_comment'></div>亦有何功，可以当之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1243255_comment'></div>又念一世，日月如驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1243255_comment'></div>人生浮脆，未老先衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1243255_comment'></div>如我长命，在世亦稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1243255_comment'></div>若不知足，将欲何为！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1243255_comment'></div>若更不死，又待何时！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1243255_comment'></div>况营坟圹，有年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1243255_comment'></div>复与二亲，邱陇相依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1243255_comment'></div>今得归往，以慰孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1243255_comment'></div>且有精舍，在旁护持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1243255_comment'></div>花竹竞秀，泉石争辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1243255_comment'></div>魂魄时游，亦足自怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1243255_comment'></div>昔白乐天，千载所推，年龄至此，亦与世违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1243255_comment'></div>白之旷达，素为吾师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1243255_comment'></div>得与同寿，喜又可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1243255_comment'></div>寄语亲旧，不须涕洟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1243255_comment'></div>如我存没，皆过所期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1243255_comment'></div>我既无憾，尔又何悲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1243255_comment'></div>已戒儿曹，莫求挽词，亦莫称述，辄立墓碑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1243255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1243255'><span class='label'>按：</span>光绪《仙居县志》仙居集一三，光绪二十年刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1243255_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1182')">1179-1182年</a>　致仕居里。生活闲适。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　致仕居里。晚年因年岁大而眼瞎耳聋，生活不便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　是年有诗与友人唱和。作品：《和沈先觉韵》<div id='poem_101491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和沈先觉韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101491")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101491'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101491'>枉度浮生八十春，休谈天数与人伦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101491'>长贫已是难糊口，久病那堪更累身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101491'>独把新诗娱晚景，谁将灵剂起痿人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101491'>若教得酒时时醉，醉里高吟尚绝尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101491_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101491'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年4月</a>　四月，妻郭氏卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年6月</a>　六月吴芾卒，谥康肃。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年10月</a>　十月，夫妻合葬石井中奥之原。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bc2566a5eb0841c19c65c0bf0d3ac344_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc2566a5eb0841c19c65c0bf0d3ac344");'><span id='bc2566a5eb0841c19c65c0bf0d3ac344_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1132')">1127-1132年</a>，24-29岁</div><div id='bc2566a5eb0841c19c65c0bf0d3ac344' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　金掳徽、钦二帝北去，北宋亡。康王赵构在南京（今属河南）即位，南宋建立。吴芾南归客临安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年7月</a>　客临安。七月，闻宗泽薨，为诗哭之。作品：《哭元帅宗公泽》<span class='inlineComment2'>（王可喜博士论文《宋代诗人丛考》，武汉大学2014年。）</span><div id='poem_101949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭元帅宗公泽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101949")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101949'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101949'>呜呼哀哉元帅公，百世一人不易逢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101949'>堂堂天下想风采，心如铁石气如虹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101949'>正色立朝不顾死，半生常在谪籍中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101949'>真金百鍊愈不变，流水万折归必东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101949'>落落奇才世莫识，欲知劲草须疾风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101949'>维时中原丁祸乱，尘氛涨天天濛濛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101949'>众人畏缩公独奋，毅然来建中兴功。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101949'>雄图一定百废举，复见南阳起卧龙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101949'>呜呼哀哉元帅公，翩然遗世何匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101949'>无乃天上亦乏才，故促我公还帝宫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101949'>公还帝宫应有用，何忍坐视四海穷。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101949'>吁哉四海正困穷，兴仆植僵赖有公。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101949'>公虽居东都，天下日望公登庸。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101949'>公今既云亡，天下不知何时康。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101949'>正如济巨川，中流失舟航。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101949'>当今士夫岂无人，请问谁有公器业，谁如公忠良。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101949'>公虽不为相，德望震要荒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101949'>公虽非世将，威棱詟豺狼。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101949'>伟哉奇节冠今古，我试一二聊铺张。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101949'>靖康元年冬，敌人正披猖。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101949'>庙堂惊失色，愁睹赤白囊。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101949'>公首慨然乞奉使，欲以口伐定扰攘。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101949'>朝廷是时未知公，公之蚤志不获偿。<div id='poem_sentence_22_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_101949'>忧国耿耿思自效，再乞守土河之旁。<div id='poem_sentence_23_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_101949'>命下得磁州，翌日径束装。<div id='poem_sentence_24_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_101949'>下车未三日，边骑已及疆。<div id='poem_sentence_25_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_101949'>敌人闻之亟退舍，匹马不敢临城隍。<div id='poem_sentence_26_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_101949'>顷之得兵数十万，康邸赖公王业昌。<div id='poem_sentence_27_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_101949'>及公领留守，北顾宽吾王。<div id='poem_sentence_28_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_101949'>恩威两得所，春雨兮秋霜。<div id='poem_sentence_29_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_101949'>馀刃曾不劳，危弱成安强。<div id='poem_sentence_30_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_101949'>奸雄悉胆落，谁敢乱纪纲。<div id='poem_sentence_31_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_101949'>呜呼哀哉公死矣，民今有粟安得尝。<div id='poem_sentence_32_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_101949'>狙诈乘我虚，近复陷洛阳。<div id='poem_sentence_33_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_101949'>洛阳去东都，雉堞遥相望。<div id='poem_sentence_34_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_101949'>不闻敢侵犯，岂是军无粮。<div id='poem_sentence_35_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_101949'>祇畏我公霹雳手，气慑不复思南翔。<div id='poem_sentence_36_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_101949'>呜呼哀哉公死矣，秋高马肥谁与防。<div id='poem_sentence_37_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_101949'>天子久东狩，去冬幸维扬。<div id='poem_sentence_38_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_101949'>都人心恋主，谓言何相忘。<div id='poem_sentence_39_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_101949'>朝夕望回辇，断肠还断肠。<div id='poem_sentence_40_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_101949'>公独以死请，再请意愈刚。<div id='poem_sentence_41_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_101949'>呜呼哀哉公死矣，万乘何当归大梁。<div id='poem_sentence_42_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_101949'>咄咄食肉人，尚踵蔡与王。<div id='poem_sentence_43_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_101949'>奸谀蔽人主，痛<span class='inlineComment2'>（宜秋本作痡）</span>毒流万邦。<div id='poem_sentence_44_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_101949'>人怨天且怒，意气犹洋洋。<div id='poem_sentence_45_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_101949'>所冀我公当轴日，尽死此曹膏剑铓。<div id='poem_sentence_46_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_101949'>呜呼哀哉公死矣，始知国病在膏肓。<div id='poem_sentence_47_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_101949'>我公我公经济才，设施曾未竟所长。<div id='poem_sentence_48_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_101949'>但留英声与后世，永与日月争辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_49_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_101949'>此死于公亦何憾，顾我但为天下伤。<div id='poem_sentence_50_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_101949'>我闻天下哭公者，哀痛不翅父母丧。<div id='poem_sentence_51_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_101949'>父母生我而已耳，岂能保我身无殃。<div id='poem_sentence_52_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_101949'>邦人此时失所依，波迸东下纷苍黄。<div id='poem_sentence_53_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_101949'>我公我公不复见，秋风在处生凄凉。<div id='poem_sentence_54_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_101949'>百身傥可赎，我愿先以微躯当。<div id='poem_sentence_55_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_101949'>灵丹傥可活，我愿万金购其方。<div id='poem_sentence_56_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_101949'>彷徨愧无起公计，安得长喙号穹苍。<div id='poem_sentence_57_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_101949'>呜呼哀哉元帅公，太平时节君不容。<div id='poem_sentence_58_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_101949'>及至艰难君始用，民之无禄天不容。<div id='poem_sentence_59_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_101949'>呜呼哀哉元帅公，古来有生皆有终。<div id='poem_sentence_60_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_101949'>唯公存亡系休戚，千年万口长怨恫。<div id='poem_sentence_61_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_101949'>嗟我草茅一贱士，念此抑郁气拂胸。<div id='poem_sentence_62_101949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_101949'>衔哀挥涕何有极，愿以此诗铭鼎钟<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《湖山集》卷四）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_101949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月</a>　来信知故居紫丁香盛开，有诗咏怀。作品：《得家书报敝居紫丁香盛开怅然有感》<div id='poem_101966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>得家书报敝居紫丁香盛开怅然有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101966")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101966'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101966'>我家丁香大盈丈，天公靳惜非凡材。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101966'>去年花开香满屋，我方局促缠悲哀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101966'>准拟今年必无事，尽可花下相追陪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101966'>何期顿与花隔绝，斗粟牵从江上来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101966'>前日我家寄书至，为报堂前花正开。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101966'>熏人已如兰麝喷，照眼还若锦绣堆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101966'>狂蜂游蝶自来往，旧成蹊处今生苔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101966'>主人有花不解赏，向来何以事栽培。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101966'>置书不觉双泪堕，人事好乖如此哉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101966'>嗟我行年近六十，鬓发星星心已灰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101966'>纵使从今得自便，此生看花能几回。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101966'>况复奔驰未能已，断蓬正滚风中埃。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101966'>欲往一见尚不可，敢望近前持酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101966'>须知轩冕傥来耳，不如归去山之隈。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101966'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_101966_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年5月</a>　五月，权尚书户部侍郎。<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年9月</a>　同月，罢宣谕司，为参赞军事。作品：《辞宣谕奏状》<div id='poem_1243249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞宣谕奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_1243249")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243249'>臣一介疏远，陛下过听，付臣以淮西之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243249_comment'></div>臣退惟江淮表里之雄，师旅营屯之众，事大体重，受任匪轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243249_comment'></div>臣学不知兵，才非应猝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243249_comment'></div>究淮西之形势，实江左之藩篱，列城云屯，诸将环峙，内以宣昭于王略，外以安静于边陲，是必精神足以折冲，智识足以应变，始可当一面之重寄，宽九重之顾忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243249_comment'></div>如臣懵不习于军旅，愚亦闇于事机，倘冒宠荣，必辜任使。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1243249_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年9月</a>　是月，转左朝议大夫，洪适草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年11月26日</a>　十一月二十六日，除敷文阁直学士知临安府，充两浙西路安抚使，洪适草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　是年有诗与王之望唱和。作品：《王瞻叔参政寄惠云笈经因成四韵奉酬》<div id='poem_101321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
