id='poem_content_101321'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101321'>老来犹未返林泉，终日区区亦可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101321'>拟扣玄关求至道，喜披云笈探真筌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101321'>他时使我离尘境，今日由君结妙缘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101321'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　是年有诗挽汤思退。作品：《挽汤丞相三首》<div id='poem_101673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>挽汤丞相三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101673'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101673'>平步青云上，逢辰亦盛哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101673'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101673_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_101672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101672'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101672'>游刃有馀地，孤忠不愧天。<div -----title
乐清

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101968'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101968'>晚学愧淹博，微官妨隐盘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101968'>攀龙荣请事，敛板喜承颜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101968'>懦庸资盼睐，簿领洗尘烦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101968'>南丰茂人杰，才望蔼江关。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101968'>题舆裨德政，镇俗念时艰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101968'>仙山寻胜外，妙句落人间。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101968'>气连天柱壮，清夺霜空寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101968'>一读三叹息，发立谁敢谩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101968'>但嗟俊逸才，尚滞海之湾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101968'>中兴急贤哲，日日闻赐环。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101968'>况复有如公，骥足宁久閒。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101968'>会须早命驾，即日当召还。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101968'>发硎观利器，断鳌新海寰。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101968'>宣室伫前席，顾问应夜阑。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101968_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101968'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_101968_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101967?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_101967'>高才独立万夫却，险语磨崖山鬼愕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101967'>翕然万口竞流传，一字谁能加笔削。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101967'>自怜庸钝百不聪，晚来喜见人中龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101967'>更看挥翰光夺目，恍如海蜃浮青红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101967'>一时闻望已难攀，相见平居养浩然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101967'>慷慨胸襟包海岳，轩昂高义薄云天。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101967'>散材不谓蒙知遇，孤迹何期遂保全。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101967_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101967'>碌碌未能酬国士，正惭他日尉通泉。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和何倅游雁荡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101866")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101866'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101866'>何侯富词藻，能赋兼能诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101866'>百篇辈<span class='inlineComment2'>（宜秋本作卑）</span>李白，十稔嗤左思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101866'>搜奇抉灵怪，造化不能私。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101866'>每为山水游，锦囊随所之。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101866'>雁荡閟神秀，鬼物潜司巇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101866'>开林发幽隐，肇自兴国时。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101866'>高岩耸崷崒，列岫森瑰奇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101866'>龙湫神光异，龙鼻灵液滋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101866'>天柱万仞立，冰帘千丈垂。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101866'>羡君沿檄来，暇日遂遍窥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101866'>兴随佳处发，景与高情宜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101866'>留步欣有得，过眼光如遗。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101866'>乘寒蹑危磴，跻险攀樛枝。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101866'>雅有许询兴，心形不知疲。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101866'>我渐动拘俗，薄宦方栖迟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101866'>恨君为此行，不获相追随。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101866'>平生爱山心，自视如调饥。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101866'>寻幽傥有路，初不问险夷。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101866'>几欲老山间，便将云衲披。<div id='poem_sentence_18_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_101866'>顷幸官是邑，柴车日载驰。<div id='poem_sentence_19_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_101866'>列贤不暂舍，游燕必于斯。<div id='poem_sentence_20_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_101866'>每欲状奇怪，苦乏幼妇词。<div id='poem_sentence_21_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_101866'>千岩与万壑，胸中徒自知。<div id='poem_sentence_22_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_101866'>别来岁月久，况复逢艰危。<div id='poem_sentence_23_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_101866'>兹虽值平时，老大无所施。<div id='poem_sentence_24_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_101866'>今观君所赋，妙境俱在兹。<div id='poem_sentence_25_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_101866'>慨然想云壑，应不谓我欺。<div id='poem_sentence_26_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_101866'>会当寻旧游，重与同襟期。<div id='poem_sentence_27_101866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_101866'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_101866_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在温州乐清县尉任上。夏日同官会饮白鹤寺双瀑亭，有诗纪之。作品：《夏日同官会饮白鹤寺双瀑亭李道济作诗纪事因次其韵》<div id='poem_101950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101950' class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101950")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101950'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101950'>嗟予好泉石，所至穷幽胜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101950'>年来堕尘埃，复苦炎热盛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101950'>赖有古招提，相去不步仞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101950'>何时供燕游，庶以息喧竞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101950'>山僧结虚亭，潇洒净如镜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101950'>双瀑从天来，景物更幽迥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101950'>栏楯溢波光，清凉殊可凭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101950'>复幸僚友贤，雅与山川称。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101950'>贰邑不负丞，所蓄金玉润。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101950'>耿侯固坦夷，赵子亦纯正。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101950'>盍簪已足乐，况复有名酝。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101950'>酒酣人意适，坐久天宇静。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101950'>踏月各言归，清风远相趁。<div id='poem_sentence_14_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_101950'>君诗继踵来，敏捷过于瞬。<div id='poem_sentence_15_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_101950'>中复含妙理，不独写幽兴。<div id='poem_sentence_16_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_101950'>读罢愈惊人，痴坐不知暝。<div id='poem_sentence_17_101950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_101950'>援笔强续貂，安能继高咏。<div 丽水

ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101490")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101490'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101490'>心地荒芜旷几春，朅来邂逅共耕耘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101490'>交情正喜清如水，归兴那知去似云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101490'>百首漫劳频寄远，一樽终拟再论文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101490'>胡为竟尔乖前约，寂寞车音杳不闻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101490_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101490'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　是年在当涂，有诗述怀。作品：《题碧云亭》<div id='poem_101983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题碧云亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101983")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101983'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101983'>累土创新亭，本拟还旧观。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101983'>或言旧亭庳，视此才及半。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101983'>我方安朴拙，岂敢事轮奂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101983'>言念梦幻身，终日困几案。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101983'>既未许自如，超然脱羁绊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101983'>亦欲对江山，时发一笑粲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101983'>自从得新亭，顿觉百忧散。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101983'>亭前柳色新，亭下荷花乱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101983'>明月可坐邀，积雪堪俯玩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101983'>凭栏送飞鸿，千里归一盼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101983'>诗成似有神，酒行欲无算。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101983'>取次亦足乐，胡为尚兴叹。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101983'>恨吾年已衰，志不在游宦。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101983'>何当归去来，终老湖山畔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101983'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_101983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　是年在当涂，有诗与友人唱和。作品：《次韵沈漕使寄和碧云亭之作》《和蒋无退咏雪》<div id='poem_101835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵沈漕使寄和碧云亭之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101835")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_101835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101835'>衰年厌尘劳，久念作净观。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101835'>奉祠还故山，阅岁更过半。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101835'>草草结茅庐，虽无轮与奂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101835'>水作绿罗衣，山为青玉案。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101835'>自足了馀生，岂谓浮名绊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_101835'>牵从江上来，去国同王粲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_101835'>既与猿鹤疏，还惊鸥鹭散。<div id='poem_sentence_6_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_101835'>公馀坐危亭，四顾云影乱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_101835'>新诗忽鼎来，累日饱吟玩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_101835'>洗我胸中尘，宛如睹清盼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_101835'>信知隐侯家，句法有成算。<div id='poem_sentence_10_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_101835'>方今苦乏材，当馈屡兴叹。<div id='poem_sentence_11_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_101835'>如公人物英，宁久从远宦。<div id='poem_sentence_12_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_101835'>会见御追风，起自长淮畔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_101835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_101835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_101835_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/101561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和蒋无退咏雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_101561")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_101561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_101561'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_101561'>腊中三白几年无，今岁呈祥事可书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_101561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101561'>披得一蓑方入画，翻成双带又随车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101561'>共惊飞絮迷清昼，更觉同云满太虚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101561'>忆昔读书灯火少，喜穿窗牖映吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101561'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　是年，在当涂编李之仪《姑溪集》五十卷，锓板于学，并作序。作品：《姑溪集序》<div id='poem_1243251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1243251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姑溪集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25062, "宋", "吴芾", "poem_title_1243251")'>吴芾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1243251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1243251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243251'>李公端叔以词翰著名元祐间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243251_comment'></div>余始得其尺牍，颇爱其言思清婉，有晋宋人风味，恨未睹他制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243251_comment'></div>乾道丁亥，假守当涂，因访古来文士居此邦而卓然有声于世者，惟李太白、郭功父与端叔三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243251_comment'></div>郡旧有太白、功父集而端叔独缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243251_comment'></div>求于其家，而子孙往往散落，无复遗稿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243251_comment'></div>间得之邦人，类而聚之，命郡士戴翚订正，釐为五十卷，锓板于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243251_comment'></div>昔二苏于文章少许可，尤称重端叔，殆与黄鲁直、晁无咎、张文潜、秦少游辈颉颃于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1243251_comment'></div>今观其文，信可知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1243251_comment'></div>或谓端叔晚节锐于进取，有所附丽，虽若可疑，然范忠宣公遗奏极于鲠切，诋斥不顾，一时用事者欲置忠宣之子于理，端叔慨然自列，谓实出其手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1243251_comment'></div>既而公所为忠宣行状复出，由是得罪南迁，废锢终身，曾不少悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1243251_comment'></div>其勇于义若此，讵可以微瑕掩之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1243251_comment'></div>余固爱其文，又表其行谊之可嘉者，并以诏于后云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1243251_comment'></div>端叔名之仪，其先景城人，既谪而南，始居姑溪，自号姑溪居士，今以名其集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1243251_comment'></div>天台吴芾序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1243251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　知太平州。有善政。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_101291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101291'>偶驱千骑出，还得十朋来<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：时有十客。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101664'>过雨江山新似洗，连天草树翠成堆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101664'>搜罗好景归诗句，断送閒愁付酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_101664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_101664'>对此愿公拚一醉，相逢能得几回来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_101664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_101664'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_101664_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_101663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_101663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_101663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_101663'>恨居平地去天远，喜上高台与月亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年10月</a>　十月，为太平州郡廨作题名记。作品：《续题名记》<div id='poem_1243253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1243253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1243253'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1243253'>郡廨旧阙题名，绍兴二十二年，炜公直阁来守是邦，始命立石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1243253_comment'></div>仅记建炎以后守臣名氏，其登载为未详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1243253_comment'></div>余以乾道三年至此，更加采访，得诸父老，谓绍圣以来，自吕希哲、黄庭坚、梅灏、王景修、王资、韩宗直、霍汉英、徐绩、何昌言、乐昭厚、唐秷、陆蕴、刘会元、单炜、徐禋、周需、范洎、臧祐之接于沈思者凡十有八，正兵火之馀，其爵序岁月漫不可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1243253_comment'></div>惟张伯玉嘉祐四年以侍御史来，独见于所刻《祭李翰林》之文，其词致清逸，犹可想其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1243253_comment'></div>其馀以图籍不存，莫可概见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1243253_comment'></div>余惜其无传，因刻诸副石之首，以昭于后云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1243253_comment'></div>乾道四年十月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1243253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1243253'><span class='label'>按：</span>乾隆《（安徽）太平府志》卷三四，乾隆二十二年刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1243253_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_101842'>令尹若能终此意，清风着处会知名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_101842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_101842'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_101842_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌
